< Review>
My mom is 69 and unfortunately has neglected her teeth for most of her life. As a young girl she had a horrible experience at a dentist office and developed a fear of dentists. The combination of this fear and of course putting her children's care over her own lead to the deterioration of her teeth. I knew her teeth were bad but it wasn't until she lost one of her front teeth and we made a trip to the dentist that I really understood the severity of her situation.

We went to a "traditional" dentist and walked away with close to a years worth of appointments. I knew right then that this process would never work. I could possibly get my mom to the first and maybe even the second appointment but after that it would be a struggle.

That is when my family found Clear Choice. My brother and I went to a seminar to learn more about this company, the procedure and if in fact it was true that someone could walk away with a new set of teeth . Well, it was TRUE.

I cannot express in this review what Clear Choice has done for my mom. When she first visited Clear Choice she weighed all of 95lbs, if that. We realized that without most of her teeth and the poor condition her remaining teeth were in she was not able to eat solid foods and was not getting proper nutrition. To imagine my mom not being able to bite into a apple or eat a steak or even something as easy as bite into a sandwich was heartbreaking. Clear Choice was not just a clear choice for my mom, it was the ONLY choice!

The entire staff at Clear Choice, San Diego is amazing! From the greeters at the front desk, Ryan Peterson who has been with us from day one and goes out of his way to check on my moms progress each visit to the outstanding doctors who performed my moms miracle. Scott Perkins, DDS and Arshiya Sharafi, DDS, PC we so caring and gentle with my mom. We would not be where we are today without the care of this team!

My mom is now complaining that her clothes do not fit, we have gone up a few sizes and can't seem to fill her appetite. Dream Come True! Clear Choice gave my mom her smile back but more importantly gave my mom her life back and you cannot put a price tag on that! Thank you Clear Choice!<//Review>

< review>
Pho and donuts? Sure, why not! Two of some of my favorite things can be found at South Swell Donuts: Pho and donuts! And it is especially comforting on a rainy day for someone visiting from out of town like myself.

It was a rainy afternoon when I turned to my trusty Yelp app to look for a pho spot in the area. Surprisingly, South Swell Donuts popped up on my feed and I began perusing this shop‚Äôs Yelp photos and reviews. I was sold after reading a few reviews and I knew I had to try it out.

South Swell Donuts is located in Laguna Beach on PCH between 2nd and 3rd. There is limited street parking in front of the shop, as well as up the hill from the corner of the street. After snagging a parking spot, I walked in with my mom and we were welcomed with a friendly, ‚ÄúHello, sweetheart!‚Äù This friendly owner was Jackie and she was the sweetest lady!

We asked about their pho but, with our luck and Mother Nature, Jackie told us they had sold out of pho earlier in the day due to popular demand and the rainy weather. No worries at all because we were able to take back some donuts. Jackie recommended we try their Cronut, which we got 2, as well as some twists and Apple fritter. We also picked up some milk to drink with our donuts.

For a family donut shop, their twisted donuts are on the smaller size; however, they tasted unbelievably delicious! There is something about them that tastes a lot milkier or creamier with a fluffier batter. It is definitely not like the hollow raised donuts with just sugar ‚Äî South Swell Donuts are a step above mom-and-pop donut shop donuts. Their Cronut is definitely a MUST here! It is so dense, crispy yet fluffy and overall just good! Their donuts are not overly sweet like Krispy Kreme but they have that same melt-in-your-mouth consistency. Their donuts are not complex in flavor like Side Car Donuts but are classic in their flavors.

I was really pleased with their donuts and I definitely will stop by again the next time I‚Äôm in the area! Jackie‚Äôs customer service is enough to make you return for another visit and, hopefully, next time I‚Äôll be able to grab a bowl of their pho (rain or shine)!<//review>

< review>
I'll admit, I always thought of Little Caesars as low quality due to the low price. I've had it a few times before and decided I'd finally buy some for myself. I tried almost all of the specialties, the extra pepperoni, the baked cheese crust, and the pretzel crust with cheese sauce. < Review>
Slowly this location has bit the dust in terms of food quality and service. I have continued to go to this location for a year now and will now switch, just so I can have better consistency with my pizza.

I grew up in Michigan surrounded by Little Caesars pizza so I love the company and taste. This location however has continued to mess up called in orders, overcharged five dollars on pizza, and consistently produce terrible breadsticks.

I am not saying Little Caesars is the most gourmet pizza out there, but burnt breadsticks with no butter and very little cheese is definitely not what Mike Ilitch, the founder of LC, had imagined or produced when he started his own LC.

I hope more people stop going here because I know I am. I gave them multiple chances to get right and they just continue to disappoint.</Review>

<rating>3</rating>< text>
While the selection is great and the prices are low, the quality, overall, leaves much to be desired. Most of the shoes you'll find are some of the top brands and styles out there right now, but once on your feet, they end up feeling like the castoffs of the assembly line. I bought some nice-looking Fila's which ended up feeling like they were going to come unglued from the front immediately after putting them on. I suppose they are worth the $35- not including tax- I paid for them, provided they last me a few months, but if you care about your feet, or if you suffer from orthopedic issues, look elsewhere. "Quality over quantity" is usually my motto.< /text>
